The robot has both arms empty and is at base configuration v3, with arm configuration v5. All objects are graspable.
           
           The previous plan had an invalid `move_base` action because `v3` was not the starting base configuration in the action instance provided. The `move_base` action takes two base configurations as arguments, and a trajectory. The first argument is the current base configuration, and the second is the target base configuration. We also need to specify the base trajectory that connects these two base configurations. For instance, if the robot is at `v3` and wants to move to `q4`, the valid action is `(move_base v3 #q4 #o0)`. The error indicated `(move_base v3 #q4 #o0)` was invalid. Looking at the list of valid actions, indeed `(move_base v3 #q4 #o0)` is not listed, but `(move_base v3 #o0 #q4)` is not listed either. The initial state is `atbconf(v3)`. It seems like `o0` is a base trajectory, and not a base configuration. The valid action is `(move_base v3 #o0 #q4)` and not `(move_base v3 #q4 #o0)`. This implies that `o0` must be a base trajectory connecting `v3` and `q4`. Similarly, `o3` is a base configuration. So for a move action from v3 to q4, the action would be `(move_base v3 #o0 q4)`. This is not correct for this problem; from the given action list, the second argument of the `move_base` action is a base trajectory. In the list, the action form is `(move_base <base_config_1> <trajectory> <base_config_2>)`. The current base configuration is `v3`. The target base configuration for picking v8 is `q4`. The trajectory connecting `v3` to `q4` is `t53`. So the action should be `(move_base v3 #t53 q4)`.
           
           The plan needs to explicitly include `move_base` actions to transition between the initial base configuration `v3` and the base configurations required for `pick` and `place` actions. The `kin` facts indicate the base configuration for each `pick` and `place` action.
           Specifically:
           - To pick `v8` from `v9`, the required base configuration is `q4`. The initial `atbconf` is `v3`. We need a `move_base` from `v3` to `q4` using trajectory `t53`.
           - To place `v8` on `#o2`, the required base configuration is `o3`. We need a `move_base` from `q4` to `o3` using trajectory `o0`.
           - To pick `v16` from `v17`, the required base configuration is `q9`. We need a `move_base` from `o3` to `q9` using trajectory `o0`.
           - To place `v16` on `#o2`, the required base configuration is `o3`. We need a `move_base` from `q9` to `o3` using trajectory `o0`.
           - To pick `v12` from `v13`, the required base configuration is `q7`. We need a `move_base` from `o3` to `q7` using trajectory `o0`.
